The Hubei Flood Relief Association sent a public telegram stating: "To the Shanghai City Party Headquarters, the Municipal Government, the Shanghai Office of the Central Relief Commission, the Public Security Bureau, and all newspapers: We have just received a telegram from the relief office in Shanghai stating, 'We have received your telegram. We immediately convened a meeting of all the committee members and named it the Shanghai Relief Office of the Hubei Flood Relief Association. Mr. Jiang Yuxu was publicly elected as the chairman of the committee. The office is temporarily located at 78 Gongshun Lane, Wuma Road. Please inform the Party and municipal authorities in Shanghai to take note and file it for record. We hereby report this matter and respectfully request your attention.' Our association resolved at the tenth standing meeting to establish relief offices in Nanjing and Shanghai. We have already telegraphed the fellow villagers in Shanghai. Now, in accordance with the previous request, in addition to sending telegrams to other parties, we are sending a special telegram to you, hoping that you will take note and file it for record and provide assistance at any time. We wish you success. Hubei Flood Relief Association."

Dredging Bureau Sends Ship to Gaoyou 120

Song Ziliang, Director of the Dredging Bureau, has been making great efforts to help with this flood disaster. In addition to sending gasoline pumps to Wuhan to carry out pumping work, he also sent Deputy Engineer Xue of the bureau on the Haiying ship from Shanghai to Gaoyou at 10:00 AM yesterday to help the victims.

Efforts from All Walks of Life to Help with Disaster Relief 121

▲ Youzheng Bookstore Donates 3,000 Yuan The Youzheng Bookstore on Wangping Street held a three-day sale at a low price to help with disaster relief. However, due to the rainy weather, only 720 yuan was sold. The owner, Di Chuqing, made up the difference to 3,000 yuan, sending 1,000 yuan to the Disaster Relief Associations of various provinces and the remaining 1,000 yuan each to the Jiangsu Charity Relief Association and the Liyang Flood Relief Association.

▲ Egg Industry Concludes Fundraising After Raising a Large Sum The committee members of the Egg Industry Association have raised a large sum of money through the enthusiastic donations of their members. A total of 10,245.5 yuan in cash, 150 taels of silver, and 4 dimes in small foreign currency have been received. After sending the money to various relief organizations, they will hold a closing ceremony.

▲ Meeting of the Clothing and Bedding Disaster Relief Association The Clothing and Bedding Disaster Relief Association held a meeting at 4:00 PM yesterday at its general office at 207 Mengdelan Road. Those present included Lu Jianai, Cai Nipei, Shang Mujiang, Jiang Xiahun, Fan Fayuan, Chen Kuitang, Ni Songlin, Huang Chunzhou, Zhu Caiyin, and dozens of others. The meeting began at 5:00 PM, and Lu Jianai was elected as the temporary chairman and Zhu Caiyin as the secretary. First, Mr. Huang Chunzhou reported on the progress of the association, explaining that the public has been enthusiastically donating cotton-padded clothes in large numbers, reaching thousands of pieces. Chairman Lu proposed that the association's expenses should not be covered by external donations. Chairman Lu and Cai Nipei and others first donated 100 yuan each. It was decided that the fundraising methods would be divided into manual and written publicity to implement the work. The Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce Boy Scout Corps also sent a representative, Mr. Wang Yingqi, to the meeting, hoping that members would be willing to volunteer for publicity work. The meeting adjourned at around 7:00 PM.

▲ Municipal Staff Members Donate Meal Savings for Disaster Relief The municipal committee members and related personnel of this city have formed a dining club that meets once every two weeks. There are currently more than 30 members. They take turns hosting a week every five months. The other day, the members of the association had dinner at the Dajiali Restaurant on Beijing Road. Mr. Yang Bingxing proposed that since the flood disaster is so severe, we should not abolish our dining club, as it is related to the discussion of official matters. However, we should tighten our belts and donate the savings to disaster relief. Each time, three people can save 30 yuan. If we calculate by week, we can get more than 300 yuan. The money should be donated first to provide relief to the flood victims in Jiangsu Province on a weekly basis until the end of the disaster relief. It was decided that each person would first donate 10 yuan as a week's savings. The money will be brought to the next dinner meeting. Wang Binyan was appointed as the cashier. If the disaster does not subside, a second week of donations will be considered.

▲ Taikang Company Jointly Donates 200 Yuan The colleagues at the Nanjing Road branch of Taikang Company contributed 10% of their September salaries and the Mid-Autumn Festival feast money, totaling 200 yuan, which has been entrusted to Liu Jingchuan to be handed over to the relief agencies.

▲ Shenchang Foreign Firm's Chinese Employees Donate More Than 1,000 Yuan The Chinese Employees' Association of the American firm Shenchang Foreign Firm raised a total of 1,075.56 yuan in donations from the firm's employees for the flood disaster. The money has been sent to the Publicity Group for transfer to the Jincheng Bank.

▲ Central Hotel Employees Donate 311 Yuan Shen Changgeng, the assistant manager of the Central Hotel on Wuma Road, raised 311 yuan in donations from the hotel's employees for disaster relief, which was submitted to the Disaster Relief Association yesterday for distribution.

▲ Qiuxin Workers Donate to Help Disaster Relief The Qiuxin Office of the First District Shipbuilding Industry Union convened a meeting of all group leaders at 5:00 PM yesterday and resolved that each worker would donate half a day's wages to help with disaster relief.

Labor Disputes Involving French Tram Workers Expand 122

Tram Service Suspended Yesterday

French Concession Under Temporary Martial Law

Union Asks Company for Forgiveness

Seven Workers Sentenced to Imprisonment

Workers at the French Concession Electric Light Company were connecting a power line at the home of a Mr. Gao at No. 5 Shenyu Lane, Huacheng Road, at 11:00 AM the day before. Because they leaned a bamboo ladder against the back door of No. 4, a dispute arose with Li E'e, a woman from Ningbo living in No. 4. Then, at 5:30 PM, the workers invited more people to take revenge, which led to a major disturbance in front of the Songshan Road police station. Since the case occurred, all trams in the French Concession have been declared on strike since 9:00 PM the night before. Therefore, all public buses and trams on the roads of the French Concession were completely suspended yesterday. The French police paid great attention and dispatched Chinese and Western police officers on duty, all armed, to protect the area. The iron gates on the road from Xiaodongmen to Xieqiao on the Republic Road were all closed, leaving only small doors for traffic. The details are summarized as follows:

▲ Workers Go on Strike More than 1,200 workers in more than 20 departments of the French Concession Water and Electricity Company's Mechanical Department, including the lathe, tap water engineering office, painters, fire meter connection, large warehouse, carpenters, motors, and Dongjiadu water engine railroad, went on strike together at 6:30 AM yesterday to support the arrested workers.

▲ Demanding Bail The Second District Water and Electricity Industry Union (i.e., the French Concession Water and Electricity Mechanical Department) sent representatives Lu Guanhong, Zhang Renjun, Qiao Lingen, and Zheng Deshun to the company yesterday morning to negotiate with the director, Meng Suolang, demanding that the company bail out the arrested workers Zhu A'long, Yu Haiquan, Cao Liang, and Chen A'xi. The director said that it was not a matter for the company and that he could not interfere, so he had to wait for the Second Special District Court to resolve it.

▲ Workers' Congress All the workers in the Mechanical Department held a congress at the company at 275 Luban Road at 11:00 AM yesterday. The chairman was Zhang Yinsheng. First, Zhang Renjun reported on the negotiations with the director. Due to time constraints, the chairman announced that the meeting would continue at 1:00 PM in the afternoon. However, all the workers insisted on demanding the release of the arrested workers. By the afternoon, the company had closed the factory gates and stationed a large number of armed detectives, so the meeting could not be held.

▲ More Arrests The French Concession Water and Electricity Company closed the factory gates in the afternoon due to the workers' strike and stationed Chinese and Western armed detectives. After the workers finished lunch, they prepared to enter the factory to work, but because the factory gates were closed, they could not enter and temporarily went to the union to await orders. At 2:00 PM yesterday afternoon, Zhu A'san, a worker in the machine shop of the Mechanical Department, was arrested in Lujiawan and taken to the Lujiaqiao police station.

▲ Mediation in Progress The Second District Water and Electricity Union held a discussion meeting at the union yesterday afternoon. Zhang Yinsheng, Zhang Renjun, Lu Guanhong, and Qiao Lingen were sent to ask Du Yuesheng to mediate at 4:20 PM. As a result, all the workers returned to work first, and the rest would be investigated. The company would not refuse the workers to return to work. The union would prepare a letter to the company and the police station to clarify everything.

▲ Statement of Misunderstanding The Second District Water and Electricity Union sent a letter to the French Concession Water and Electricity Company yesterday, stating, "Dear Director, this unfortunate incident was caused by a small matter that escalated into a dispute. It was a misunderstanding by the workers. In order to resolve the matter, the person in charge of our union has notified everyone to return to work together and await a resolution. We hope that you, the director, will forgive us. Sincerely, Tram Company Director." A letter was also sent to the Songshan Road police station to clarify the misunderstanding.

▲ Announcement of Resumption of Work The Second District Water and Electricity Union announced the resumption of work yesterday afternoon, stating, "Regarding the dispute, the representatives are negotiating with Mr. Du Yuesheng, who has accepted the mediation. All our workers will resume work as usual on Monday. The night shift workers in the old and new workshops, engine rooms, and Dongjiadu will work as usual tonight (i.e., yesterday)." Therefore, the night shift workers entered the factory to resume work at 6:00 PM.

▲ Court Judgment The arrested workers Zhu A'long, Yu Haiquan, Cao Liang, Chen A'xue, Gao A'fu, Zhao Jinsheng, and Chen Baobao were escorted to the Second Special District District Court by the police station yesterday. The criminal court president, Ge Zhitan, together with prosecutor Ding Shikui and clerk Chen Weihan, sat in the criminal court for interrogation and announced that the case was serious and that all onlookers were prohibited. Judge Ge first asked the defendants their names, ages, and native places. Then, Fei Xizhen, the police station's lawyer, stood up to state the case, saying that the case arose from the fact that the electric light company sent craftsmen Chen Xiangyun and A'mao to connect a power line at the home of a Mr. Gao at No. 5 Shenyu Lane, Huacheng Road, at 11:00 AM yesterday morning. They leaned a bamboo ladder against the back door of No. 4. However, the alley was narrow, and Li E'e, a woman living in No. 4, was going out to buy things. She thought that the bamboo ladder was leaning against the door and blocking traffic, so she asked them to move it. However, the workers not only ignored her but also teased her. The two sides got into an argument, and the workers even slapped Li E'e in the face, which angered the neighbors who took sides and beat the three workers. The workers were humiliated and unwilling to accept this, so they took advantage of their time off work at 5:00 PM and invited more than 100 workers to look for trouble at No. 4 Shenyu Lane, Huacheng Road. At that time, Li Genfa, Li E'e's brother, who worked at the Dalei Foreign Firm, came home from work and saw this situation. He asked the workers for the reason, but the workers did not ask questions and beat Li. Li saw that the situation was not good and fled into the building at No. 32 Huacheng Road, climbed over the fence from the sun deck into another house, and escaped. At that time, the workers scattered. One of the workers grabbed Li's raincoat and walked to the Quan'an Teahouse on Baxianqiao. The victim, Li Genfa's friend Zhuang Zifa, caught a glimpse of him and reported it to the Songshan Road police station, which immediately dispatched three Chinese police officers, No. 370, No. 340, and No. 675, to the Quan'an Teahouse to arrest him. However, the workers beat the police officers again. At that time, only three workers, including Li Hesheng, were arrested and taken to the police station. They were interrogated and released because they were not related to the case. Unexpectedly, more than 200 workers rushed to the Songshan Road police station, intending to forcibly release the arrested workers. The workers were fierce and aggressive. At that time, the victim Li Genfa arrived at the police station gate by car and was beaten by the workers again. The chief of the Criminal Department, the Western detective Bao Erdi, the Russian detective Dula Cai Fu, and the Western patrol head No. 61 were also injured. Patrol head No. 61 drew his gun and fired two shots into the air for self-defense. At that time, the chief patrol Feiwoli and the tram company director were also at the scene. Seeing this fierce situation, they ordered the police to disperse the workers by force and arrested the seven defendants one after another. Now, the police station is prosecuting them for obstructing official duties under Article 143 of the Criminal Law, disrupting order under Article 156, gathering a crowd for robbery and coercion under Article 157, demanding release by violent acts under Article 171, and obstructing traffic due to others under Article 202. Then, the plaintiff Li Genfa was interrogated. He stated that he was 24 years old, from Ningbo, and lived at No. 4 Shenyu Lane. He worked at the Dalei Foreign Firm. When the workers had a dispute with his sister yesterday morning, he was at work, so he did not know the situation. It was not until 3:00 PM that his sister called to inform him. He came home from work at 5:00 PM and saw many workers at the alley entrance. He went forward to ask, but they beat him with iron rods without asking questions, saying that they would kill him. Fortunately, he saw that the situation was not good and fled into the building at No. 32, climbed over the fence from the sun deck into No. 18, and escaped. However, he had been seriously injured all over. He had been examined at the Blue Cross Society, and there was a medical report to prove it. However, when he was beaten, he lost a raincoat and 30 yuan in cash. Li E'e stated that she was 16 years old. Yesterday morning, three workers were connecting a line at No. 5 next door, and they leaned a bamboo ladder against the back door. When the woman went out to buy coal balls, she asked them to move the ladder. However, the workers not only refused but also threw mud at her and teased her at will. At that time, the woman reasoned with them, and they scolded her as a slut and slapped her in the face. The woman was humiliated and fled home. Later, others saw this and beat the workers. When the workers left, they said that they would come back for revenge later. Unexpectedly, at 5:00 PM, more than 100 workers came to seek revenge and rushed into her house first. Fortunately, the woman fled into the front building and was not beaten. Later, the woman heard that her brother was being beaten by the workers on the road, so she tried her best to go out and wanted to take a car to report to the police station, but she was also stopped and beaten by the workers. There were injuries that could be proven. The judge asked the defendants if they were the perpetrators at the scene. Li E'e pointed out that the first defendant, Zhu A'long, was the one who beat her. Then, the witness Zhuang Zifa was interrogated. He stated that he was a merchant and worked in a customs brokerage. Li Genfa was his friend. Yesterday afternoon, the merchant went to Li's house because of something, but Li had not yet returned. After a while, he heard that Li Genfa was being beaten by the workers at the alley entrance. When the merchant went out to rescue him, the workers had all fled. The merchant only saw a worker carrying Li Genfa's raincoat and walking north. He followed him, intending to find an opportunity to report to the police. He then saw the worker go to the Quan'an Teahouse to sip tea. Therefore, the merchant reported to the police station and dispatched the police to go with the merchant to arrest him. However, the workers were extremely rude and dared to commit violence again, beating the merchant and the police together. The merchant's waist was injured from the beating. He requested an examination. The judge asked which of the workers in the case were the perpetrators at the scene. The answer was that the first defendant, Zhu A'long, was indeed the perpetrator who beat Li E'e. At this point, the judge ordered the forensic doctor Wei Ligong to take the three plaintiffs to the back rest room for examination. Then, Dr. Wei reported that Li Genfa and Zhuang Zifa had indeed been injured, which was consistent with the medical report from the Blue Cross Society. As for the injury suffered by the woman Li E'e, it could not be examined for the time being because the plaster was applied. According to the head of the Western patrol No. 61, he was ordered to mobilize the entire reserve team of patrol officers at the Songshan Road police station at 6:00 PM yesterday to disperse the crowd. However, the workers refused to obey and surrounded him, trying to seize his gun. Therefore, he got an opportunity to draw his gun and fire into the air to defend himself, but his finger was also injured by the workers. According to Bao Erdi, the head of the Criminal Department, he had submitted a written report, but his injuries were very minor. According to the Chinese patrol officers No. 370, No. 340, and No. 675, they were ordered to go with Zhuang Zifa to the Quan'an Teahouse to arrest the workers, and they were all beaten. The defendant Zhu A'long stated that he and the craftsman Zhu Xiangyun were colleagues. After leaving work at 5:00 PM yesterday, he was invited by Xiangyun to go to the Quan'an Teahouse to drink tea. Later, he heard that his colleagues had been arrested by the police station, so he went to the police station gate to inquire and was arrested. Yu Haiquan stated that he was a craftsman in the electric light company. After leaving work at 5:00 yesterday, he went to Quan'an to drink tea and was arrested by the Vietnamese police while passing by the Songshan Road police station. Cao Liang stated that he was a tap water worker. After going to Quan'an to drink tea at 5:00 PM yesterday, he heard that the workers had been arrested, so he went to the police station gate to watch and was arrested. Chen A'xue stated that he was also a worker in the electric light company. He was arrested while passing by the Songshan Road police station on his way home from work yesterday. The judge asked, "Is it your decision that the tram is not running today?" They all replied that they did not know. Zhao Jinsheng, Gao A'fu, and Chen Baobao stated together that they were blacksmiths in the Industrial Bureau's motor room. After receiving their wages at the Industrial Bureau yesterday afternoon, they went to the Quan'an Teahouse to shake a club because a new car had been arrested for no reason. Therefore, they went to the police station gate to watch and did not dare to cause trouble. They did not know the workers of the electric light company. The two lawyers, Jin Yu and Li Yuan, were also appointed to argue that the court had already inquired about the case and that the three defendants Zhao Jinsheng, Chen Baobao, and Gao A'fu were all eating tea at the Quan'an Teahouse. Others had committed the beating, so they requested that they be declared innocent. At this point, Judge Ge announced the end of the debate and issued a verdict in court. Zhu A'long was sentenced to six months of imprisonment for publicly gathering a crowd to obstruct official duties and two months of imprisonment for jointly injuring others, with a total sentence of seven months of imprisonment. Yu Haiquan was sentenced to six months of imprisonment for publicly gathering a crowd to obstruct official duties. Cao Liang and Chen A'xue were each sentenced to two months of imprisonment for publicly gathering a crowd to obstruct official duties. Zhao Jinsheng was sentenced to two months of imprisonment for jointly injuring others. Gao A'fu and Chen Baobao were each sentenced to two months of imprisonment for publicly obstructing official duties. The number of days of detention before the judgment was finalized was counted as two days for one day. Zhao Jinsheng, Gao A'fu, and Chen Baobao were all given a two-year suspended sentence and ordered to be released on bail at any time. If they could not provide bail, they would be detained.

▲ Letter Requesting Severe Punishment The Ningbo Shanghai Fellow Villagers Association learned from the villagers' report yesterday that the case was related to local security and that the situation was extremely serious. After the special commissioner investigated the matter thoroughly, an emergency meeting was convened to discuss methods to assist the victimized fellow villagers. As a result, in addition to comforting the victim Li Genfa, letters were sent to the Shanghai Second Special District District Court and the French Concession General Police Station, demanding that the culprits in this case be severely punished in accordance with the law to appease public anger.

Local News

Shanghai's Continuous Rain and Wind 123

Yesterday, Water Accumulation Was Widespread Again

Rice, Grains, and Vegetables Were All Affected

This year, the amount of rainfall in this city is particularly high. Since the hurricane and heavy rain on the 26th of last month, water has accumulated everywhere, damaging walls, houses, and trees, almost leading to a rare disaster. Fortunately, after days and nights of wind and rain, the sky suddenly cleared. However, general transportation and power lines have been obstructed. Unexpectedly, since the beginning of this month, on the morning of the 4th, the sky was suddenly covered with dark clouds, and the north wind gradually increased. By the afternoon, the rain poured down again, and as of last night, it had not stopped for a single moment. Therefore, in the low-lying areas of the concession and the Chinese city, coupled with the inadequate drainage of the ditches, water has accumulated to a foot deep. The conditions in various places are recorded as follows:

▲ Conditions in the Concession Along the western roads of the Public Concession and the Rue Lafayette and Rue Bayle of the French Concession, pedestrians wearing rain boots could not pass easily. At the intersection of Route Saipoise and Avenue Joffre, the accumulated water was a foot deep, and vehicles splashed water everywhere as they passed. However, this rainfall was not as severe as the previous one, so many coolies temporarily earned money by carrying pedestrians on their backs.

▲ South City Submerged The Chinese city in the South City, after the heavy rain of the previous two days, was a vast expanse of water, turning into a swamp. Low-lying areas such as the Local Court, Huining Road, Guohuo Road, Xin Puyu Tang Road, Daxing Street, and Shangwen Road were all knee-deep in water. The Local Court was surrounded by water on all sides, and the lower-level staff inside the court were working barefoot. The water of the Huangpu River has reached the shore, and pedestrians are also wading through the water.

▲ Zhabei's Plight Due to the continuous heavy rain, low-lying areas in Zhabei, such as near the Meigen Road Station, behind the Jiajun Guild Hall, in front of the Xijin Public Office, and north of Datong Road and Gonghe Xin Road, open spaces have all become a vast expanse of water. Along the roads of Zhonghua Xin Road, Pusan Road, and Hu-Tai Road, the grass sheds are submerged in water to varying depths of one or two feet. Datong Road, from the Zhijiang Temple Road south to the Zhonghua Xin Road section, about half a mile long, has turned into a river. The grass sheds in the water, viewed from a distance, are no different from islands in the ocean. Thousands of impoverished people from Jiangbei live in the water every day, with no way to change their situation.

▲ Slight Increase in Rice Prices Rice merchants also temporarily suspended opening their bins due to the rain in the past two days. However, according to inquiries at various retail rice shops, the highest grade of white rice, which had previously fallen from 20 yuan to 17 yuan per picul, was sold yesterday at 17 yuan 8 jiao or 18 yuan per picul, exceeding the price limit by about one yuan. However, this grade of white rice is now stored in the inner rooms, and not all ordinary households can buy it. The commonly sold first and second grades of white rice are replaced with the second and third grades, respectively, and the price is increased. The recorded rice prices for yesterday are as follows: First-grade white rice (replaced by second-grade white rice) 17 yuan per picul, second-grade white rice (replaced by third-grade white rice) 16 yuan 4 jiao per picul, new japonica rice 16 yuan, bian yuan (glutinous rice) 15 yuan 6 jiao, foreign indica rice 16 yuan, mechanical indica rice 14 yuan 8 jiao, and guest indica rice 14 yuan.

▲ Shortage of Vegetables Due to the continuous cloudy and rainy weather, most of the cotton, rice, vegetables, and other crops planted in the rural areas around this city have been damaged by flooding. The heavy rain poured down the night before last, without stopping all night, and the water level rose sharply. Although the various vegetables planted by nearby farmers were available on the market yesterday morning, the prices have doubled. The vegetables in various vegetable markets, such as cabbage, edamame, loofah, gai choy, chives, etc., were obstructed by the heavy rain. Although prices rose, goods were still scarce.

▲ Collapsed House Injured People The house at No. 130 Yanhai Road, Yunjie Street, inside the Old North Gate, is the property of the Silk Industry Association. Its rear wall facing the street, due to being soaked by wind and rain, suddenly collapsed at 1:20 PM yesterday. A woman named Chen Shen, who lived at No. 4 Yuchang Lane in Shizi Lane, happened to be passing by and was seriously injured in the head and right leg by the collapsed wall. A rickshaw puller named Yuan Zhilin happened to be passing by at the time and was also injured in the right leg, hip, and arm. The police officers arrived and immediately took the injured people to the Second District, First Branch Police Station, and then transferred them to Renji Hospital for treatment. The collapsed wall was more than two zhang long. Afterwards, the association called the Public Works Bureau and asked them to send workers to surround the remaining collapsed wall with wooden frames to prevent it from collapsing again and injuring people.

Jiangnan Embankment Works Office Seizes Time to Repair Seawalls 124

The Situation Is Mostly Free of Danger

Reports have been made in this newspaper about the dangerous situations and emergency repairs of the seawalls in Baoshan and Taicang counties. It is now learned that Director Xue Zhaoshu of the Jiangnan Embankment Works Office immediately rushed to block the breaches day and night after the dangerous situations occurred at Xuejiatan in Baoshan and Daotangmiao Wangjiazhai in Taicang. The progress was very fast. Yesterday, he accompanied the engineers and others to Daotangmiao Wangjiazhai in Taicang in the rain to direct everything. It is reported that the office has made proper arrangements for the preliminary emergency rescue project plan and implementation steps. It is also reported that the report submitted to the Provincial Construction Department and Water Conservancy Bureau is roughly as follows regarding the engineering aspects: (1) The dangerous works plan is to add hemp bags to the rammed earth and add stone outside. (2) The project personnel and administrative arrangements are as follows: Assistant Engineers Feng Dan and Mou Tongbo are stationed in Baoshan Xuejiatan to be responsible for the dangerous works in Baoshan. Zhang Tingnan and Zhang Bin are stationed in Taicang Daotangmiao to be responsible for the dangerous works in Taicang. (3) Material purchase situation: More than 1,000 pieces of local materials in Taicang have been transported, and 13,000 to 14,000 hemp bags have been transported. In addition, 200 cubic meters of Jiangyin stones have been purchased, and ten boats have arrived. In Baoshan, it is planned to purchase 4,000 pieces of wood first, and 1,000 pieces have been transported. It is planned to purchase 60,000 hemp bags first, and 10,000 have been transported. Another 10,000 can be transported today. (4) Material transportation situation: In Taicang, cars are used from Shanghai to Liuhe, and small carts are used from Liuhe to the construction site. During high tide, ships are used from Liuhe. In Baoshan, cars are used from Shanghai to Baoshan, and small carts are used from Baoshan to the construction site. During high tide, ships are used from the Sui Tang River. All must reach the construction site within two or three days. (5) Construction methods: The contracted price for ramming earth is stipulated to be 1 yuan 1 jiao to 2 jiao per cubic foot at the bottom, and 4 jiao 5 fen to 5 jiao per piece for the stone. Try to contract out at a reasonable price as much as possible. It is a fixed division of labor. In addition, there are one or two flying shifts for workers, which are mobile and specialize in sporadic projects (currently being organized). (6) Worker situation: There are 200 earthworkers and one shift of pile drivers in Taicang. Another shift can be added within one or two days. There are also about 200 earthworkers and two shifts of pile drivers in Baoshan. It is planned to increase the number of earthworkers by four or five hundred within two or three days. Negotiations have been completed. (7) Current status of the project: This project is arranged to start from the breaches and then the gaps, and then the secondary dangers. The breach at Daotangmiao Wangjiazhai in Taicang has been roughly 80% to 90% completed. The newly built embankment has passed the high tide level and is preparing to add pile drivers and stone construction workers. The breach at Xuejiatan in Baoshan is being done by earthworkers and stone workers at the same time and has been 50% completed. If the weather is fine for the above breach projects, it is expected that the work can be completed by the third day of the eighth lunar month. In addition, small breaches in Baoshan, such as Zhangjiazhai Niutou and Jing Wuyuedun, have also been recruited, and work will begin immediately. It is expected to be completed before the fifteenth day of the eighth lunar month. It is also reported that Director Xue plans to go to Songjiang Jinshanwei to inspect and repair emergency projects after the workers and materials in Baoshan are sufficient.

Shanghai Tuberculosis Hospital's New Hospital Construction Plan 125

The Current Hospital Affairs Are Progressing Exceptionally Well

The New Hospital Site Is on Hongqiao Road

The Tuberculosis Sanatorium at No. 2 Great Western Road in this city was established in 1928 and was founded by Huang Hanzhi and Ding Fubao. Wu Zhihui, Xu Shiying, Wang Yiting, and others are directors. German medical doctors Finashi, Ding Huikang, Huang Dinghu, Wu Zhengji, and others are the medical directors. Since its establishment, it has been highly praised by the community. It has now expanded to four hospitals with 50 single rooms. The first hospital of the hospital is the outpatient department and the X-ray department, which are open for a long time. Patients can come and have X-rays taken at any time during the consultation hours and pick up the results the day after tomorrow. This measure greatly facilitates the diagnosis of patients. The second hospital specializes in receiving patients with severe tuberculosis, so that they can be isolated from those with mild tuberculosis. It is equipped with a chemical laboratory. The hospital uses the erythrocyte sedimentation rate test to measure the prognosis of tuberculosis, the suitability of treatment, and the progress of the disease, which is extremely accurate. The third hospital specializes in receiving patients with mild tuberculosis and has a 10-foot-wide veranda for recumbent therapy. The fourth hospital is a new-style building. One wall is entirely a large window. When the sky is clear, it can be fully opened, and the bedroom is equivalent to a veranda. If the weather is bad, the windows can still be closed and the patient can lie down. Outside the window, there are fountains and waterfalls, and the flowers and trees are quiet and beautiful. There are also disinfection surgery and electrotherapy rooms, where lung surgeries such as rib resection, artificial pneumothorax, and phrenic nerve resection can be performed.

The new hospital plan of the hospital on Hongqiao Road is based on the rapid progress of the city and the original hospital site is insufficient. The site has been selected on the west side of Zhongshan Road on Hongqiao Road. The area is densely forested and the air is fresh, which is very suitable for suburban convalescence. The new hospital's design is completely based on the architecture of the Swiss White Mark Sanatorium, with a social hall, dining room, music library, rest room, Italian garden, rooftop solarium, and other facilities. The samples are being made and it is expected that they will be completed at the same time as the new municipal government building at the end of next year.

The Court Investigates the Murder Case of Xia's Servant 126

After Ling Xiangxiang, the sedan carrier of the famous doctor Xia Yingtang, was killed and burned to destroy the evidence, the local court discovered the case and has been paying unusual attention to it in recent days. Since the Xia family has strict rules, it has been determined that the deceased Ling Xiangxiang was not killed by outsiders. Therefore, the investigation has now begun, and it is expected that all employees will be severely interrogated by the court in order to find out the truth. As for Xia himself, the court will also interrogate him to determine responsibility.

Xiao Guoxiang Returns to China 127

Xiao Guoxiang, a car expert who studied in Europe and America, is 28 years old and a native of Tongcheng, Anhui. After graduating from the liberal arts department of Jinling University in 1927, he went to France to specialize in automobile manufacturing and interned at Panhard Motor Company for many years. In the winter of 1928, he went to England and tested and manufactured at famous automobile factories such as Dunlop and Morris-Sheldon in Birmingham. In the summer of 1929, he left England for the United States and went to Dodge Motor Company for an internship of two months. In the autumn of the same year, he entered the University of Michigan to specialize in the principles of automobile science and graduated the following year. In 1930, he remained in the United States to study road science. This summer, he completed his studies and returned to China. He has now arrived in Shanghai on the Empress of Japan. It is learned that Mr. Xiao has been hired by the National Road Association as an expert for the Road City Exhibition and an honorary contributor to the Road Monthly. He will return to Anhui to visit relatives within a few days and then come to Shanghai when the exhibition opens.

Engineer Yin Wenyou Returns to China After Studying in the United States 128

Mr. Yin Wenyou, a graduate of Nanyang University, is a native of Wuxi, Jiangsu. He went to the United States to study in August 1924 and obtained a master's degree in mechanical engineering and a master's degree in science engineering from Cornell and Harvard Universities. He has worked as an engineer in the US Stone Engineering Company, Horse Aircraft Factory, and Teletypewriter Company for many years. He arrived in Shanghai on the President Wilson on the 4th of this month. He is the author of a book on aircraft engineering, which will be published soon. Based on his experience, he has invented a Chinese teletypewriter, which is expected to be completed soon.

Cheng Jingyi Returns to China 129

Arriving in Shanghai on the 8th

Dr. Cheng Jingyi, President of the World Council of Churches and General Secretary of the National Christian Council of China in this city, went to the United States in early May to attend the World Presbyterian Church Conference and the World Youth Conference, and was invited to speak on Chinese church and social issues in major cities in the United States. Wherever he went, he was well received. He has now returned to China after completing his public affairs. He telegraphed yesterday that he has arrived in Japan and will arrive in Shanghai on the 8th of this month. After a short rest, he will travel to Sichuan Province.

Counterfeit Dutch Banknotes Discovered and Used 130

Long Qing and Tang Mingzong Were Both Detained

Long Qing from Guangxi took 20 ten-yuan (gold yuan) Dutch banknotes from Java Bank to Dingyu Money Shop at No. 294 Zhejiang Road and Jiujiang Road at 7 PM the day before yesterday to exchange for 340 Shanghai silver dollars. After Chen Zhibin, the shop assistant, carefully examined the banknotes, he realized that they were all counterfeit. He reported it to Chinese detective Ye Yuming, who arrested Long. After questioning, he learned that there was an accomplice, Tang Mingzong, waiting at the entrance of Wing On Company. The detective then arrested Tang and took him to the Old Gate Police Station. After investigation, it was learned that they belonged to an organized group and that there was also a person named Feng who was the instigator. Feng first opened room 55 in the Great Eastern Hotel and then handed Long Qing the 20 counterfeit banknotes and a ship ticket from Java Shipping Company, ordering him to exchange them at Dingyu. His plan was that if others detected it, he could claim that the banknotes were brought by the Dutch and that he was exchanging them because he lacked travel expenses. At that time, he would also show the ship ticket to make people believe it. Unexpectedly, it was exposed. Yesterday morning, the police station sent the two criminals, Long and Tang, to the First Special District Court Criminal Division. The police station's lawyer, Ru Baoyi, prosecuted them for counterfeiting currency in accordance with Article 212 of the Criminal Law. Because the case still needs to be investigated, a postponement was requested. When questioned, Long Qing confessed that Feng had instructed him to do it, while Tang Mingzong confessed that he knew nothing about it. Judge Xu Jiazhanshi reviewed the confession and ordered the case to be adjourned for one week. The two defendants were returned to custody.

Qinglian Pavilion's Owner and Concubine Cross-Accuse Each Other 132

Both Parties Were Found Not Guilty

A Hawker Steals His Way to Death 133

A Husband Demands Adultery Money and Is Detained - A Strange Tale

Jiang Asan, a Ningbo native, 36 years old, who lives in Rongsen Lane, Lane 2, Menggu Road, Zhabei, and runs a vegetable business, recently became entangled with a certain woman, secretly engaging in adultery more than once. Unexpectedly, joy turned to sorrow, and the matter was discovered by the woman's husband. At about 9 AM the day before yesterday, he led four or five hooligans to Jiang's house, claiming that Jiang had taken another man's wife and threatened to use force. At that time, a mediator came forward to mediate. The group initially wanted Jiang to pay 50 yuan to settle the matter, but Jiang was a poor man and had no such huge sum of money. After repeated requests, it was agreed that 10 yuan would be paid. Then, they left. Jiang immediately borrowed money from relatives and friends without success. In desperation, he thought of living together. Learning of this, he rushed to the rescue, but it was too late, and Jiang had died. At 1 PM, the woman's husband and a certain Jia came to Jiang's house to demand 10 yuan, but they were detained by the neighbors. They reported to the Fourth District Police Station, which ordered the police to arrest Jia and Yi and take them back to the police district, and ordered the local constable to report to the local court for verification.

The Story of How Wu Wang, a Woman From Baoying, Was Deceived 134

Wu Wang, a woman from Baoying, is 43 years old and has a daughter named Fenzhu, who is 25 years old this year. In 1922, Wu arranged for her daughter to marry Li Shukun, a fellow villager, through a matchmaker. Li was engaged in the South Goods industry in Liyang. After Wu's daughter, Fenzhu, married into the family, the two sides could not reconcile their opinions, and there were often disputes. In February of this year, Fenzhu had another conflict with Li over a minor matter. At that time, she felt resentment and thought that her mother was working as a servant in the Song family in Suzhou. So, she went to Suzhou, intending to divorce Li. Unexpectedly, when she arrived at the Song family, her mother was out on business and she could not meet her. Then, she took a car to Shanghai and was introduced by her younger sister to work as a servant in the family of a certain surname in Anren Lane, Kangti Road, in the French Concession. Because the work of the employer was too heavy every day, she felt that she could not bear it. Thinking that if she quit, she would have nowhere to live. Just when she was in a dilemma, Zhao Zhang, a woman from Yixing whom she knew, came to her and said that she knew a man from Wuxi named Ding Aji, who was 29 years old this year and lived at No. 85 Meijia Lane in the South City. He was engaged in the mahjong business and had a wealthy family. He was now short of a wife and wanted to find someone suitable. If she was willing, Zhao could act as a matchmaker. Fenzhu was overjoyed when she heard this and asked Zhao to help her with the introduction. On April 11, Ding Aji welcomed Fenzhu to his home and lived together, and paid 30 yuan as a reward to Zhao Zhang. After Fenzhu entered Ding's house, she realized that Ding was also a poor man and realized that she had been deceived by Zhao Zhang. She was very frustrated, but since the matter was irreversible, she could only sigh at her bad luck. After learning that her daughter had gone to Suzhou and was not found, Wu Wang immediately rushed to Shanghai to search for her daughter's whereabouts, but she had no success. So, on July 4, she returned to Suzhou, resigned from her job as a servant, and came to Shanghai again. She was introduced to work as a servant in the family of a certain surname at No. 53 Qiaojia Shed. She took time to go out and look for Fenzhu, but after two months, there was still no news. Until the day before yesterday, Wu had an important matter and was passing near the Vulcan Temple inside the Great Eastern Gate. Suddenly, she met Fenzhu on the road. Mother and daughter were overjoyed after being separated for a long time. After talking, she learned the truth and felt angry. She immediately went to Kangti Road to arrest Zhao Zhang and took her to Meijia Lane in the South City, along with Ding Aji. She reported them to police officer Wei Jin, who was guarding the Fifth Post. The precinct chief, after a preliminary hearing, ordered that the case involved the abduction of a married woman and ordered that a written report be submitted to the Shanghai Public Security Bureau for investigation.

Two Suicides 135

Both Were Due to Difficult Livelihoods

▲ Wang Zhikui Wang Zhikui, a native of Suzhou, was 30 years old. He used to be in the foreign goods business but has now lost his job. At about 2 AM the day before yesterday (the 3rd), he went to the Nanjing Hotel in Hongyun Lane, next to the Nanking Theater on Edward Road. He was led to room 12 by the tea room attendant, paid two yuan for the room, and went to bed. Two hours later, there was a sudden groan from room 12. The tea room attendant knew that something was wrong and tried to pry open the door. He saw Wang lying on the bed, his face pale. He knew that he had taken poison. He quickly reported to the accounting room and called the Songshan Road Police Station, ordering the detective to come and hire a car to send him to Renji Hospital. He died at 9:30 AM. A white linen long shirt, a straw hat, a hairnet, a pair of white canvas shoes, three copper double-hao coins, a bottle of black liquid medicine, and a small amount of medicine were left in the room. A page of foreign paper was left on the table, but the handwriting was illegible. The content was roughly that he was being pressed by livelihood and could not survive. He was temporarily borrowing the hotel as a place to die. He hoped that they would forgive him for his audacity.

▲ Zhang Agen Zhang Agen, 21 years old, a resident of No. 302 Chengdeli, Shanjia Garden, Baker Road, in the Public Concession, was a member of a military band. Recently, due to the sluggish business, his livelihood was difficult. In a moment of anger, he secretly took poison and committed suicide yesterday. Afterwards, the neighbors noticed and hired a car to send him to Renji Hospital for treatment, but it was ineffective. He died at about 1 PM the next afternoon. His body was sent by the hospital to the autopsy station to await a report to the court for inspection.

Reader Communications

Inquiry from Mr. Gu Liangcun

It has been five or six years since I graduated from the rural normal school. Because my income is not much, my economic situation has become even more difficult this summer due to my marriage. In order to solve the economic problem, I have to try to further my studies. I have decided to enter law and politics or pattern making, but I am troubled by three things: diploma, tuition, and household expenses. (It is inconvenient to enter a cram school because I live in Pudong.) Can you tell me the best way to solve this problem?

(Reply) Since you have graduated from a rural normal school, you should first serve in a rural primary school for several years, and then fully prepare both your economic and academic abilities before seeking further education. This is reasonable. At this time, when funds are difficult, it is best to seek employment first. Regarding the issue of a qualifying diploma, there will be and should not be any special methods to solve it. Law and politics and architectural design, commonly known as pattern making, are different in nature and even more different from normal school. We believe that you should examine your own nature, talent, and environment, and identify one of these types. The best (easiest) way is to specialize in education, first work as a school teacher, accumulate some experience, and then pursue further education in the future. But this requires you to seriously consider and decide for yourself.

Inquiry from Mr. Zhi Ran

I am a child from a poor family and have received elementary school education. Now I cannot earn enough and there are still parents at home who are over sixty years old and cannot work, nor is there any progress. Needless to say, what will happen in the future, all current daily expenses are my responsibility. However, what I earn is only enough for my own use, how can I bear this huge burden? Therefore, I want to find a better job, but I do not have a suitable position. Please solve this problem in the newspaper.

(Reply) It is not easy for you to find a better job, because to do that kind of job, you must first acquire that kind of knowledge and skills. To put it another way, you must also accumulate a wealth of experience in that kind of job. The higher the salary, the more professional skills are needed. Therefore, to plan for you, it is best to stick to your current job in the store and think of a way to improve. For example, if you work in the accounting room, then study accounting; if you work in the sales department, then study retail. There are books that can be studied in your spare time. Improve step by step from self-study. Others don't understand, I understand. Others can't do it, I can do it. This is how you stand out. This is called upward progress in your own field. There are many famous successful people in Shanghai who came from this background. Do not change jobs easily. The Chinese Vocational Education Society on Huanlong Road has a correspondence school to help young people study on their own in their spare time. You can ask Mr. Jin Daoyi, who is in charge.

Reader Communication Guidelines for the Shen Bao 138

The staff of this newspaper firmly believes that each of our esteemed readers has specific pressing issues that require immediate discussion. Based on the spirit of serving society, we are willing to act as consultants and offer sincere advice in written form. Should our readers thus obtain suitable solutions, alleviate their difficulties, and increase their happiness, we would be greatly gratified.

1. The questions readers wish to discuss with the staff of this newspaper are temporarily limited to three categories: education, career, and marriage.

2. When communicating, please clearly state your surname, given name, gender, age, occupation (or place of study and grade level), native place, and mailing address. (It is advisable to provide these details even when continuing correspondence, to avoid any potential undelivered mail.) Subsequently, please clearly state the problem you wish to discuss in detail and with accuracy, so that people can easily understand your true intentions. On the outside of the envelope, please write "Shen Bao Reader Communication Department, Received," and attach sufficient postage stamps for a reply.

3. When communicating, please cut out the special-issue stamp from the "Reader Communication" column of this newspaper and affix it to the upper-left corner of the stationery as a voucher.

4. The processing methods for incoming letters at this newspaper are as follows: A. We respect the reader's intentions. All letters that state a desire not to have a response published in the newspaper, or a wish not to have their name disclosed in the response, will be handled accordingly. B. If a letter does not state how it wishes to be answered, but the staff believes that answering one person would provide valuable reference for everyone, it will be disclosed in the newspaper. C. If a letter states a desire to have a response published in the newspaper, but is constrained by space limitations, we will either disclose the main points, or may be unable to disclose it at all, or may have to delay disclosure due to the issue requiring further consideration. We ask for your understanding in all such cases. However, if a response cannot be published in the newspaper, we will still reply by mail.

On the spot, it was resolved that: (1) the representatives who went to the Water and Electricity Workers' Union to request mediation by party and government agencies were acting in a private capacity and were not recognized; (2) those who disrupt strike discipline will be severely dealt with by the picket team; (3) a mass meeting will be held at 8 AM on the morning of the 6th to discuss the way forward.

▲Picket Meeting: All captains and members of the picket team held a general meeting at 10 PM the night before and resolved: (1) to specify the duties of the general captain and division captains; (2) that members must obey the orders of the captains; (3) that the working hours will be from 8 AM to 12 noon, 1 PM to 6 PM, and 8 PM to 10 PM daily; (4) to warn the ticket inspectors that if they do not obey, force will be used. Grounded German Ship is Out of Danger 143

Sailing to Nagasaki for Repairs

Heavy Losses of Ship and Cargo

The accident involving the German merchant ship Bachenland of the Heinrich Podeus & Co has already been reported in this newspaper. It is now learned that after the accident, the company immediately ordered the Ameland, which came from Europe to Shanghai, to rescue her. However, the ship is now out of danger and on her way to Japan, with heavy losses. The passengers were safely rescued. A follow-up report is provided below:

▲Two Cabins Flooded: This time, the Bachenland was carrying goods from Dagu, Qingdao, and other ports, and was heading to Kobe, Japan. When traveling on the sea near Korea, it hit a reef near Baojie Island. The bottoms of the first two cabins of the ship were punctured by the reef, and seawater flooded the two cabins, causing great damage to the goods. Fortunately, the cabins were separated by bulkheads, so the other cabins were not affected and the ship did not sink.

▲Passengers Rescued: After the ship accident, the Shanghai office was preparing to send a ship for rescue, and had negotiated with Jardine Matheson to send a tugboat, and ordered an employee to go along for inspection. Then, a telegram came to Shanghai from a Japanese ship, saying that after the Bachenland ran aground, the Dalian-bound postal ship Baikal Maru of the Osaka Company happened to pass by the area at around 7 PM and went to help. Twenty-five Western passengers on the German ship who were on a trip to North China and East Asia were quite frightened after the accident. They lowered the lifeboats of the Baikal Maru and rescued the twenty-five passengers, sending them to Kobe, and then taking another ship back to Shanghai. The travel expenses were paid by the Heinrich Podeus & Co.

▲Self-Rescue: Yesterday morning, the Shanghai office received a telegram from the Japanese branch, saying that after the Bachenland ran aground, fortunately the wind was calm. At around 11 PM that night, the shipowner Mr. Duniak tried every possible means and pulled the ship off the reef by himself. After temporarily plugging the holes in the bottom of the cabin, he immediately sailed to Nagasaki that night to unload the cargo from the first and second cabins and repair the ship in Japan.

▲Postponement of Export: The damage to the ship's hull and the water damage to the cargo will be evaluated after the ship returns to Germany. Now, the ship is being temporarily repaired in Japan. The ship was originally scheduled to come to Shanghai on the 11th to load more cargo for export. Now, because it is impossible, all customers have been notified that the departure date to Germany must be postponed.

Zhaoxing Ship Being Towed 144

Five Passengers Rescued Yesterday

The Zhaoxing ship of the Zhaoxing Company, coming from Yingkou to Shanghai, ran aground due to avoiding wind in the Shidao Bay of Qingshantou, as reported in yesterday's newspaper. It is now learned that the ship cannot be rescued for the time being. The company has asked the Japanese Salvage Company for help. The accurate information obtained yesterday is detailed below:

▲Front Cabin Damaged: The location of the Zhaoxing ship accident is at 122 degrees, 29 minutes, and 22 seconds east longitude, and 34 degrees, 55 minutes, and 10 seconds north latitude. After Zhang Jidan opened the ship away from the Shidao Reef, it ran aground on the beach along the coast. The bottom of the ship's bow was heavily damaged by the collision, and the hole was large. Seawater flooded the cabin, and the bow sank to the bottom of the sea, which may affect the entire ship. According to a telegram from the shipowner yesterday, part of the barrel oil loaded on the deck has been thrown into the sea to reduce the draft. The bow cabin is also being unloaded.

▲Ships Helping with Rescue: The Rongxing ship has already started helping the Zhaoxing at the accident site, unloading the cargo from the first and second cabins to drain the accumulated water from the cabins. The Hexing ship, carrying cement and other materials for repairing the bottom of the ship, has also arrived from Yingkou. After the cargo is cleared, the holes will be plugged. The Qingdao Northeast Fleet has also sent a warship to protect the ship.

▲Passengers Rescued to Shanghai: Five passengers from Niuzhuang were traveling to Shanghai on the Zhaoxing ship and were very anxious at the time. Later, the company telegraphed the Yuxing ship on the way to Shidao to rescue the five passengers from the Zhaoxing ship and send them to Shanghai. They arrived in Shanghai at 9 AM yesterday and landed at the Longmao pier in Pudong.

▲Japanese Ship Tows: Yesterday, the company agreed to ask the Tokyo Salvage Company of Japan to send a ship to the accident site to tow the Zhaoxing ship out of the shallows. Yesterday afternoon, the Shanghai office invited staff from Mitsui & Co., the Shanghai agent, to the Zhaoxing Company to negotiate the towing procedures and inform them of all the details of the accident.

Municipal Government Cracks Down on Stealing from Disaster Victims by Steamer Waiters 145

To be Dealt with According to Law if Defied

The Municipal Government recently received reports that steamer waiters are extorting, harassing, and making things difficult for disaster victims coming to Shanghai by boat every month. Yesterday, a special order was issued to the Social Affairs Bureau, stating that, according to reports, steamer waiters are extorting, harassing, and making things difficult for disaster victims coming to Shanghai by boat. Upon hearing this, we are deeply angered. Considering that the victims of this disaster have been displaced and their homes have been destroyed, and that they have nothing left, anyone with a conscience should be providing relief, let alone exploiting them again. Therefore, we hereby order you to quickly instruct all steamer companies, and to forward this to the respective labor unions, to earnestly warn all waiters under their jurisdiction that they must not demand anything from disaster victims seeking refuge in the future. Those who dare to disobey will be dealt with according to the law to uphold humanity and benefit the victims. This is the order. After receiving the order, the Social Affairs Bureau sent letters to the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company and the Shanghai Shipping Trade Union, stating that it is reasonable to make every effort to protect the disaster victims from all provinces coming to Shanghai. However, according to reports from disaster victims from Jiujiang, Hankou, and other places, such as Laoyang Bai and Li Zuomei, who came to the bureau one after another, the waiters on the boat demanded all kinds of things from them, not only taking away all of their meager living expenses, but even stripping them of their clothes, leaving them hungry and naked, and requesting relief. After reviewing the above statements, although they may not be entirely credible, the unanimous voices suggest that they are not fabricated. This kind of brutal act is not only unscrupulous and unreasonable, but also a cause for concern for the morality and the hearts of the people. Therefore, we hereby request you to investigate and instruct your subordinates to comply accordingly. If there are any who persist in evil, they will be severely punished and will not be tolerated.

At around 10:30 yesterday morning, three robbers suddenly arrived at No. 1227 Hart Road. Two were wearing white shirts and trousers, and one was wearing a dark-colored long gown. One of the robbers showed a pistol, prohibiting anyone from making a sound, and said, "Please help us today." They then confined the mistress of the house and the servants in one room. One robber was on guard outside the door, and the other robbers went upstairs and entered the room, using iron tools to pry open the cabinet doors and smash the leather boxes. They stole all the valuable ornaments and clothes, estimated to be worth about 2,400 yuan. The robbers then left. Afterwards, the victim reported the case to the Jing'an Temple Police Station for investigation.

Letters to the Editor

To the Editor: Upon reviewing the section concerning the public memorial for Dean Tan published in your esteemed newspaper on the 4th of this month, the original text of the elegiac couplet sent by our department, "Building tombs resembles the Qilian Mountains, together we admire the mourning and glorify the red land," was erroneously printed as "together we admire the mourning and glorify the red shadow," which is quite incomprehensible. Therefore, we respectfully request a correction. Your kind attention to this matter would be greatly appreciated. Sincerely, The General Affairs Office of the Songhu Garrison Command. September 5th.

To the Esteemed Editor of Shen Bao: Having read the news about the public bus strike in your esteemed newspaper, it stated, "All the ticket sellers sent five responsible representatives to the Water and Electricity Workers' Union the night before, requesting the standing director of the union to go to the Social Affairs Bureau of the Municipal Party Committee to request assistance and mediation," which is quite inconsistent with the facts. Our colleagues announced the strike because the drivers could not act in unison. Although the situation remains as isolated as before, and the attitude of the management remains as tough as before, our colleagues deeply believe in our own strength and know that the only way to achieve victory is to persist together. As for going to the Water and Electricity Workers' Union the night before to request assistance from the standing director of the union, it was the action of only three or five individuals and does not represent the opinion of the whole. The general assembly did not make such a resolution, nor did the strike committee make this decision, and no responsible representatives were sent for negotiations. This matter is of great importance. We hope that you will make a correction. Respectfully, The Shanghai British Public Bus Workers' Strike Committee. September 5th.
